## ğŸ¤” What is Nano Banana Pro?

**Nano Banana Pro** is Google's latest multimodal AI model featuring:

- ğŸ¯ **Multimodal Understanding** - Process text, images, and video
- ğŸ¨ **High-Quality Generation** - Photorealistic to artistic styles
- âš¡ **Fast Iteration** - Quick edits and variations
- ğŸŒˆ **Diverse Styles** - From pixel art to oil paintings
- ğŸ”§ **Precise Control** - Detailed composition and lighting
- ğŸ“ **Complex Scenes** - Multi-object, multi-character rendering

ğŸ“š **Learn More:** [Nano Banana Pro: 10 Real Cases](https://youmind.com/blog/nano-banana-pro-10-real-cases)

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

The portrait of the person is on the left, the text on the right. The text occupies two-thirds of the image and the portrait one-third, with a slight gradient transition effect on the portrait.
```

### No. 2: Premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

Create an Infographics with bento grid 8 module layout, user can specify any product name in Food, Medicine, tech etc category, choose language, Background style, Hero grid style

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Input Variable: [insert product name]
Language: [insert language]

System Instruction:
Create an image of premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules (card 2 to 8 show text titles only).
1) Product Analysis:
â†’ Identify product's dominant natural color â†’ "hero color"
â†’ Identify category: FOOD / MEDICINE / TECH
2) Color Palette (derived from hero):
â†’ Product + accents: full saturation hero color
â†’ Icons, borders: muted hero (30-40% saturation, never black)
3) Visual Style:
â†’ Hero product: real photography (authentic, premium), 3D Glass version [choose one]
â†’ Cards: Apple liquid glass (85-90% transparent) with Whisper-thin borders and Subtle drop shadow for floating depth and reflecting the background color
â†’ Background stays behind cards and high blur where cards are [choose one]:
  - Ethereal: product essence, light caustics, abstract glow
  - Macro: product texture close-up, heavily blurred
  - Pattern: product repeated softly at 10-15% opacity
  - Context: relevant environment, blurred + desaturated
â†’ Add subtle motion effect
â†’ Asymmetric Bento grid, 16:9 landscape
â†’ Hero card: 28-30% | Info modules: 70-72%
4) Module Content (8 Cards):
M1 â€” Hero: Product displayed as real photo / 3D glass / stylized interpretation (choose one)in beautiful form + product name label
M2 â€” Core Benefits: 4 unique benefits + hero-color icons
M3 â€” How to Use: 4 usage methods + icons
M4 â€” Key Metrics: 5 EXACT data points
Format: [icon] [Label] [Bold Value] [Unit]
FOOD: Calories: [X] kcal/100g, Carbs: [X]g (fiber [X]g, sugar [X]g), Protein: [X]g, [Key Vitamin]: [X]mg ([X]% DV), [Key Mineral]: [X]mg ([X]% DV)
MEDICINE:Active: [name], Strength: [X] mg, Onset: [X] min, Duration: [X] hrs, Half-life: [X] hrs 
TECH:Chip: [model], Battery: [X] hrs, Weight: [X]g,[Key spec]: [value], Connectivity: [protocols]
M5 â€” Who It's For: 4 recommended groups with green checkmark icons | 3 caution groups with amber warning icons
M6 â€” Important Notes: 4 precautions + warning icons
M7 â€” Quick Reference:
â†’ FOOD: Glycemic Index + dietary tags with icons
â†’ MEDICINE: Side effects + severity with icons
â†’ TECH: Compatibility + certifications with icons
M8 â€” Did You Know: 3 facts (origin, science, global stat) + icons
Output: 1 image, 16:9 landscape, ultra-premium liquid glass infographic.
```

### No. 5: New Year's Day Special: Four-Panel Puzzle for 2026 Blessing

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed multi-panel prompt for Nano Banana Pro, creating a 2x2 grid photo collage where a single female character, in four different outfits and settings, pieces together a puzzle that spells '2026 New Year's Day Happy' in the center. The prompt specifies precise facial feature retention, clothing details, background elements, and photographic parameters for a fashion magazine style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Key: Maintain precise facial features, retain original face structure, the character in the image must be completely consistent with the uploaded reference image] High-end photo studio 2x2 grid photo. Top-left panel (Navy Blue background): The character wears a navy blue uniform-style dress, decorated with gold buttons, vintage curls with a blue beret and pearl earrings. She holds up a huge puzzle piece (top-left piece, with the number "20" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center of the frame. Her eyes are focused on the central puzzle area, her expression is serious, with a slight smile. The background features navy stripes, an anchor, and the text "Set Sail for the New Year". Top-right panel (Cherry Blossom Pink background): The same woman wears a pink lace dress, a pearl necklace, a princess hairstyle with a pink rose hairpin and crystal earrings. She holds up the top-right puzzle piece (with the number "26" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle seam, her expression is focused and expectant, and her body leans forward. The background features pink cherry blossoms, the text "Beautiful Encounter", butterflies, and petals. Bottom-left panel (Mint Green background): The same woman wears a mint green cotton and linen dress, in an artistic style, with natural long hair, a green hairband, and wooden earrings. She holds up the bottom-left puzzle piece (with the text "New Year's Day" on it) with both hands, moving it upwards to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle, her expression is serious, and her mouth is slightly pursed. The background features green plants, the text "Hope Grows", new sprouts, and leaves. Bottom-right panel (Lemon Yellow background): The same woman wears a yellow dress with a sunflower pattern, pigtails with yellow bows. She pushes in the last bottom-right puzzle piece (with the text "Happy" on it) to complete the puzzle. The four pieces perfectly form the complete pattern "2026 New Year's Day Happy" in the center of the frame. She tilts her head back, looking at the completed puzzle, her face beaming with a successful, joyful smile. The center of the frame bursts with golden light and confetti. The background features a yellow sun, the text "Complete Success", smiley faces, and sunflowers. The puzzle pieces converge from the four corners to the center to form a complete picture. Clear makeup, bright ring light, 85mm lens, f/1.8 aperture, four-panel composition with puzzle interaction, fashion magazine style.
```

</div>

### No. 6: Vintage Patent Document for an Invention

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt designed to generate an image of a vintage United States patent document from the late 1800s. ### No. 8: Detailed mirror-selfie otaku room scene

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A very detailed Nano Banana prompt describing a female mirror selfie in a blue-toned otaku computer corner, with full specifications for character, environment, lighting, camera, and negative prompts.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
### Scene
Mirror selfie in an otaku-style computer corner, blue color tone.

### Subject
* Gender expression: female
* Age: around 25
* Ethnicity: East Asian
* Body type: slim, with a defined waist; natural body proportions
* Skin tone: light neutral tone
* Hairstyle:
    * Length: waist-length hair
    * Style: straight with slightly curled ends
    * Color: medium brown
* Pose:
    * Stance: standing in a slight contrapposto pose
    * Right hand: holding a smartphone in front of her face (identity hidden)
    * Left arm: naturally hanging down alongside the torso
    * Torso: body leaning slightly back; waist and abdomen exposed
* Clothing:
    * Top: light blue cropped knit cardigan, top two buttons fastened; a blue French-style bra faintly visible
    * Bottom: denim ultra-short shorts, with a blue satin ribbon bow on each side of the hips
    * Socks: blue and white horizontal striped over-the-knee socks
    * Accessory: a blue cute mascot phone case

### Environment
* Description: bedroom computer corner seen through a wall-mounted mirror
* Furnishings:
    * White desk
    * Single monitor showing a soft blue wallpaper (no readable text)
    * Mechanical keyboard with white keycaps on a blue desk mat
    * Mouse on a small blue mouse pad
    * PC tower on the right side with blue case lighting
    * Three anime figures on or near the PC tower
    * A poster of a pagoda on the wall
    * Cat-shaped desk lamp with blue accents
    * A transparent glass of water
    * A tall green leafy plant by the window (on the left side of the frame)
* Color replacement: replace all originally pink elements (clothes and room decor) with blue tones (baby blue to sky blue/periwinkle blue).

### Lighting
* Light source: daylight coming from a large window on the left side of the camera, through sheer curtains
* Light quality: soft, diffused light
* White balance (K): 5200

### Camera
* Mode: smartphone rear camera shooting via the mirror (no portrait/bokeh mode)
* Equivalent focal length (mm): 26
* Distances (m):
    * Subject to mirror: 0.6
    * Camera to mirror: 0.5
* Exposure:
    * Aperture (f): 1.8
    * ISO: 100
    * Shutter speed (s): 0.01
    * Exposure compensation (EV): -0.3
* Focus: focus on the torso and shorts in the mirror image
* Depth of field: natural smartphone deep depth of field; background clearly visible with no artificial blur
* Composition:
    * Aspect ratio: 1:1
    * Crop: from the top of the head to mid-thigh; include the desk, monitor, PC tower, and plant in the frame
    * Angle: slightly high angle from the mirrorâ€™s point of view
    * Composition note: keep the subject centered; to avoid wide-angle edge distortion, have her stand a bit further away and crop to a square later.

### Negative prompts
* Any appearance of pink/magenta anywhere
* Beauty filters/over-smoothed skin; poreless skin look
* Exaggerated or distorted anatomy
* NSFW, see-through fabrics, wardrobe malfunctions
* Logos, brand names, or readable user interface text
* Fake portrait-mode blur, CGI/illustration feel
```

### No. 9: Edo-period Ukiyo-e reinterpretation of a modern scene

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly-structured image prompt to depict a modern-day scene reimagined as an Edo-period Japanese Ukiyo-e woodblock print, with detailed guidance on anachronistic tech, composition, texture, and color.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A Japanese Edo-period Ukiyo-e woodblock print. The overall feeling is a surreal collaboration between masters like Hokusai and Hiroshige, reimagining modern technology through an ancient lens.

**The scene:** {argument name="modern scene" default="a busy Shibuya scramble crossing"}

**Edo transformation logic:**
Characters wear Edo-era kimono but perform modern actions. All technology is transformed into surreal Edo equivalents:
* Smartphones are glowing, illustrated paper scrolls being read intently.
* Metro stations and trains are giant articulated wooden centipede carriages shuffling through crowds.
* Skyscrapers are reimagined as endless, towering wooden pagodas reaching into dramatic clouds.
* Robots and mecha appear as giant, armored woodblock golems.

The composition uses a flattened perspective with large, bold, hand-carved ink outlines. The background features heavily stylized Ukiyo-e wave patterns and dramatic, swirling clouds, with a distant Mt. Fuji visible on the horizon.

The image must look like a physical print, not a digital painting.
* Texture: strong visible wood grain texture and rough paper fibers throughout the piece.
* Printing imperfections: pigment bleeding is evident. Simulate hand-pressed plates with slight color misalignment for authenticity.
* Color palette: strictly limited to traditional mineral pigments, with dominant use of Prussian blue, vermilion red, and muted yellow ochre.
* Lighting: soft, flat, shadow-free lighting with no digital gradients.

Aspect ratio is 3:4 vertical poster. Include vertical Japanese calligraphy describing the scene and a traditional red artist seal stamp in a corner.
```

A structured JSON prompt for generating a candid, intimate mirror selfie portrait of a young woman (Josephine Langford reference) in a luxurious marble bathroom. It requires strict adherence to a provided reference photo for the face.

```
{
  "image_generation_request": {
    "meta": {
      "type": "photograph",

      "aspect_ratio": "implicit portrait/vertical due to mirror selfie format"
    },
    "subject": {
      "demographics": "Young woman, slim and delicate build",
      "face_reference_constraint": {
        "instruction": "Strict adherence to the provided reference photo. The generated image must use this exact face, maintaining identity, facial structure, and the specific calm, thoughtful expression without any changes."
      },
      "appearance": {
        "skin": "Very fair, natural freckles visible across face and shoulders",
        "hair": "{argument name="hair color" default="Light red"} color. Styled in a loose, slightly messy updo with soft strands falling around the face, giving a natural, just-finished look."
      },
      "expression": "Calm, thoughtful, subtly introspective. Relaxed lips, gently focused eyes looking at phone screen. Face turned slightly to the side.",
      "pose": "Captured from the waist up, slightly angled body. One hand rests lightly over the towel across her chest; the other holds a smartphone.",
      "attire": {
        "garment": "Plush mochi bath towel secured across the chest.",
        "accessories": "Smartphone with a light-colored patterned case."
      }
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Luxurious marble bathroom, upscale hotel-like atmosphere.",
      "architectural_details": "Warm beige marble walls, large mirror, glass shower enclosure, sink counter with reflective surfaces, classic bathroom fixtures, detailed ceiling, clean lines.",
      "background_elements": "Reflections in mirrors and surfaces, bathroom fixtures."
    },
    "cinematography": {
      "shot_type": "Mirror selfie frame.",
      "framing": "Waist-up, slightly angled.",
      "lighting": "Soft warm lighting from overhead fixtures and a wall-mounted lamp. Creates a gentle glow on skin, highlighting collarbones and features without harsh shadows.",
      "color_palette": "Warm and neutral: creamy whites, soft beiges, muted gold tones.",
      "mood": "Calm, intimate, luxurious, private, natural, quietly confident."
    }
  }
}

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured JSON prompt for generating an ultra-photorealistic, 8K raw photo of a young woman taking a high-angle POV selfie. The prompt focuses on a playful, cheeky expression (winking, tongue sticking out), specific hair and apparel details (golden blonde hair, oversized cream linen shirt), and technical specifications simulating a wide-angle smartphone lens in warm, high-contrast morning light.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "prompt_structure": {
    "subject": {
      "demographics": "Young woman, early to mid 20s, fair complexion",
      "features": {
        "hair": "Light golden blonde hair, voluminous and softly tousled, worn down with signature curtain bangs framing the face, sunlit highlights catching the light",
        "eyes": "Warm brown eyes, right eye winking, left eye open and looking directly at the camera",
        "face": "Playful, flirty expression with softly raised cheeks, smooth yet natural skin texture with a gentle rosy flush",
        "mouth": "Bright smile with teeth visible, tongue playfully sticking out to the side, classic cheeky pop-star energy"
      }
    },
    "apparel": {
      "upper_body": "Oversized, pale cream or buttery yellow button-down shirt",
      "fabric": "Textured linen or black cotton gauze, slightly wrinkled, translucent quality in bright light",
      "styling": "Casual loungewear style, buttons done up to mid-chest, loose fit"
    },
    "pose_and_action": {
      "type": "High-angle POV selfie",
      "posture": "Kneeling on a bed, leaning slightly forward toward the lens",
      "limbs": "One arm extended holding the camera (out of frame), other arm resting straight down with hand pressed into the soft mattress",
      "dynamic": "Candid, energetic, spontaneous movement"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Bedroom or hotel room interior",
      "foreground": "White, plush duvet/bed sheets with realistic folds and compression from weight",
      "background": " blurred wooden nightstand, neutral beige walls, hint of a lamp and personal items, soft domestic setting"
    },
    "lighting": {

      "quality": "High contrast sunlight creating rim lighting on hair (halo effect) and distinct soft shadows on the face and neck",
      "tone": "Warm, golden hour or bright morning ambiance"
    },
    "camera_specifications": {

      "lens": "Wide-angle smartphone lens simulation (approx 24mm or 28mm)",

      "focus": "Sharp focus on facial expression"
    },
    "style_and_mood": {
      "vibe": "Playful, intimate, silly, carefree, 'woke up like this', goofy aesthetics",
      "aesthetic": "Naturalism, Gen Z selfie style, soft-focus background, clean core"
    },
    "tech_specs": {
      "quality": "Ultra photorealistic, 8k resolution, raw photo style",

    }
  }
}

No retouching, no smoothing, no beauty filters. ### No. 32: Social Media Post - High-Fashion Cinematic Portrait with Shutter Drag Effect

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt for generating a dramatic, high-fashion cinematic portrait of a woman (Sadie Sink likeness) wearing a black velvet gown. The key feature is the use of monochromatic deep red studio lighting and a 'shutter drag' or long-exposure effect to create an ethereal motion blur trailing behind the subject's face.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
"A high-fashion cinematic portrait of a woman with wavy auburn hair, wearing a deep-V neck black velvet gown. The scene is drenched in a monochromatic {argument name="lighting color" default="deep red"} studio light. A 'shutter drag' or long-exposure effect creates a ghostly, ethereal motion blur trailing to the right of her face. She has a poised, high-glance expression with bold red lipstick. One hand is gracefully touching her neck, showing a statement ring. Moody, dramatic shadows, 8k resolution, shot on 35mm lens, fashion editorial style."
>
Breakdown of Details
| Element | Description |
|---|---|
| Lighting | Saturated red monochromatic lighting with high contrast (Chiaroscuro effect). |
| Technical Effect | Shutter Drag / Motion Blur: The "ghosting" effect behind the head suggests movement during a slow exposure. |
| Subject | A woman with fair skin, freckles, and wavy {argument name="hair color" default="ginger/auburn"} hair. |
| Wardrobe | A minimalist, elegant black dress with a plunging neckline that contrasts sharply against the red background. |
| Composition | Medium shot, centered, with a soft-focus vignette that draws attention to the face and hands. |
Tips for Customizing
 * To change the mood: Replace "deep red" with "electric blue" or "neon emerald" for a different vibe.
 * To change the model: You can specify "shorter hair," "different ethnicity," or "alternative clothing" while keeping the "motion blur" and "monochromatic light" tags to maintain the style.
```

### No. 44: Infographic / Edu Visual - Nano Banana Pro Prompting Strategy for Stable Output

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

This is a comprehensive set of 10 instructions and strategies for writing effective prompts for Nano Banana Pro (Gemini 3 Pro Image), aimed at stabilizing output and avoiding garbled text. It emphasizes switching to 'Thought Mode' or 'Pro Mode', using descriptive sentences instead of keyword lists, specifying subject/background/atmosphere, and using positive language and English keywords for quality.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
â‘  Always switch the mode to 'Thought' or 'Pro' (I feel 'Thought' is better)
â‘¡ 'Describe the scene in sentences' rather than listing keywords
â‘¢ Specify the subject, background, and atmosphere as a set of three points
â‘£ Don't aim for perfection in one go; apply 'gradual corrections'
â‘¤ Avoid negative expressions; give instructions in positive sentences
â‘¥ Add quality keywords (4K, high resolution) in English
â‘¦ Clearly state the purpose at the beginning (e.g., "{argument name="purpose" default="Diagram for a proposal"}")
â‘§ Exclude unnecessary elements using negative prompts
â‘¨ Do not attempt complex edits all at once; proceed in segments
â‘© Save frequently used prompts as templates
```

### No. 62: YouTube Thumbnail - Candid Urban Street Photography Prompt (JSON Structure)

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A structured JSON prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate a highly realistic, candid urban street photograph. It describes a young woman walking on a city sidewalk, holding a coffee cup, wearing layered clothing (leather jacket, sweater vest), and specifies camera settings (selfie-style, 28mm wide-angle) to achieve a cozy, cinematic street mood with earthy tones.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

{
  "image_generation": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "young woman walking alone on a city sidewalk",
      "pose": "holding a takeaway coffee cup in one hand and a small paper bag in the other, arm slightly extended as if filming herself",
      "expression": "calm, thoughtful, slightly introspective",
      "gaze": "looking downward"
    },

      "hair": {
        "color": "dark brown",
        "style": "messy bun with loose strands"
      },
      "face": {
        "skin_tone": "fair with natural complexion",
        "makeup": "minimal, natural makeup"
      },
      "accessories": [
        "silver over-ear headphones"
      ]
    },
    "outfit": {
      "top": "white collared shirt layered with beige sweater vest",
      "outerwear": "{argument name="jacket color" default="brown"} leather jacket",
      "bottom": "blue denim jeans",
      "footwear": "casual sneakers"
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "urban residential street",
      "background_elements": [
        "red brick apartment buildings",
        "black iron railings",
        "sidewalk scaffolding",
        "city pathway"
      ],
      "weather": "overcast"
    },
    "props": {
      "drink": "white takeaway coffee cup with lid",
      "bag": "small brown paper bag"
    },
    "lighting": {
      "type": "natural daylight",
      "direction": "overhead ambient light",
      "quality": "soft and diffused"
    },
    "camera": {
      "angle": "slightly high angle, selfie-style",
      "framing": "medium shot",
      "lens": "28mm wide-angle",
      "depth_of_field": "moderate, background slightly blurred"
    },
    "aesthetic": {
      "style": "urban lifestyle photography",
      "vibe": "cozy, candid, cinematic street mood",
      "color_palette": "earthy tones, browns, muted reds, neutral grays"
    },
    "quality": {
      "realism": "highly realistic",

The viewer is holding a flashlight, creating a single circular beam of light while the rest of the space is engulfed in darkness. In the flashlight beam, it is visible that the character is positioned as if it was left behind after filming: [POSITION: lying on the floor/curled up in a corner/leaning against a table/slumped against a wall]. The character must appear completely lifeless and inactive: no action, no intentional pose, no sense of presence. If it is a doll or a costume, there must be no visible hands, rods, strings, or person inside.

The character appears old, dirty, and abandoned: worn fabric, accumulated dust, stains, discoloration, flattened or damaged areas.

The environment is clearly abandoned: dusty surfaces, old filming equipment, cables scattered on the floor, faded signs or set decorations.

Dust particles float within the flashlight beam; the space feels silent and untouched for years.

Photorealistic flashlight-based lighting, harsh shadows, rough textures, documentary realism, on-location shooting aesthetics, no stylization Aspect

Ratio 9:16
```

Hyper-realistic interior photography of the living room shown in the floor plan. The living room is fully furnished, and the spatial layout precisely corresponds to the floor plan: {argument name="furniture combination" default="curved sofa set, central coffee table, soft rug, warm wooden floor, neutral walls, natural light from large windows"}. Modern, comfortable, contemporary interior design, earth tones, soft light, realistic materials, and life details.

Right half should resemble a real interior photograph, while the left half maintains a clear architectural drawing. The two parts are visually aligned, clearly demonstrating the 'concept versus reality' contrast.

Style and Atmosphere

Architectural visualization meets real interior photography
Modern, warm, elegant residential design
Concise, professional, design studio presentation
Contrast from concept to realization

Lighting and Color

Left: Average lighting, neutral tones
Right: Natural daylight, soft shadows, warm highlights
Floor plan and room colors are harmoniously unified

Camera and Technical Details

Left: Top-down orthogonal view
Right: Interior wide-angle lens, eye-level perspective
High resolution, clear details, realistic textures

Negative Prompts:
Cartoon style, low detail, cluttered interior, inconsistent layout, unrealistic proportions, harsh lighting, exaggerated colors, text overlay, watermark

### No. 104: E-commerce Main Image - Two Soda Cans Product Photography Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed prompt for generating a commercial product image featuring two cylindrical cans, viewed from a low angle, emphasizing condensation, metallic surfaces, high-contrast lighting, and a deep red gradient background.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
IMAGE: Frame & Composition: The camera uses a low-angle, straight-on frontal view, positioned slightly below the subjects so the two cans rise above the horizon line; both cans are upright and vertically oriented, placed side by side with a narrow gap, occupying the central upper third of the frame; the lower edge crops into a metallic ledge that acts as a base plane, while the cans are fully visible from base to rim; the composition is symmetrical but slightly staggered in height, with the right can marginally taller in frame due to perspective; negative space dominates the upper background, reinforcing vertical emphasis and product isolation. Lighting & Atmosphere: A frontal key light, slightly elevated and centered, produces even illumination across both cans, generating dense, high-contrast specular highlights on condensation droplets; shadows are minimal and soft, indicating diffused fill from the front and sides; the moisture beads catch light sharply, suggesting a hard component within the otherwise controlled lighting setup; no atmospheric haze is present, but surface condensation creates a tactile, cold visual cue. Subject Geometry & Materiality: Each subject is a tall, cylindrical aluminum can with smooth vertical walls and rounded rims; both are coated in matte white printed labels with bold, high-contrast typography; circular color graphics are printed flat onto the surfaceâ€”{argument name="left can color" default="magenta and red"} on the left can, {argument name="right can color" default="yellow and green"} on the right can; the aluminum surfaces are covered with uniformly distributed water droplets of varying diameters, clinging via surface tension; droplets create micro-lens effects, distorting underlying text and graphics; edges are crisp, with no deformation, indicating rigid packaging. Environmental Layering: The foreground consists of a horizontal metallic ledge with linear grooves and visible fasteners, rendered in sharp focus; the cans sit directly atop this ledge, establishing physical contact; the midground is entirely occupied by the cans; the background is a uniform, out-of-focus deep red gradient wall with subtle tonal variation and no discernible texture; no additional objects or layers are present beyond these three planes. Technical Artifacts & Color: The color palette contrasts cool whites and saturated accent colors on the cans against a warm, dark red background; saturation is moderate to high in the printed circles, while the background remains subdued; fine film grain is visible across the image, especially in the darker red areas, suggesting either high ISO or intentional texture; slight vignetting darkens the frame edges; no chromatic aberration or motion blur is visible; highlights on droplets are sharp with controlled roll-off. TEXT: Title: â€œIMAGE & COMMERCEâ€; Subtitle: â€œCinematic prompt just for youâ€ (partially visible); Body: Flavor names including â€œ{argument name=\"left flavor\" default=\"Raspberry Guava\"}â€ on the left can and â€œLemon Limeâ€ on the right can; CTA: None; Logo: â€œI&Câ€; Disclaime
```

### No. 115: Game Asset - Chibi Character Operating a Cyber Window Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed, structured prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate an anime-style chibi girl operating a semi-transparent window in cyberspace. The prompt includes specific details about the character's expression, hair, AR glasses, outfit, pose, surrounding objects, background, and art style, including text overlays.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
## Overall Concept
concept: "A cute, smiling chibi character girl engrossed in operating a semi-transparent window (display) floating in cyberspace"

## Details of the Main Character
subject:
  type: "Chibi character in anime style"
  reference: "Character design should be based on the character design reference sheet attached in the image"
  expression: "A beaming smile with sparkling eyes, full of discovery and joy"
  hair:
    details: "Part of the hair faintly glows like data particles"
  wearables:
    - item: "AR Glasses"
      type: "Frameless visor style"
      material: "Highly transparent, semi-transparent material with a crystal-like texture"
      details: "The rim of the glasses glows with a thin neon blue line, projecting information into her field of view"
  outfit:
    style: "Geometric patterns resembling electronic circuits are printed in cyan on the inside of the cuffs"
  direction: "Facing the left side of the image"

## Character Action and Pose
action:
  verb: "Operating the window (display)"
  pose: "Floating gently in cyberspace, leaning slightly forward, operating the semi-transparent window (display) floating in the air"
  hands: "Lightly moving fingertips, operating the semi-transparent window (display) floating in the air"

## Surrounding Objects
objects:
  - item: "Multiple semi-transparent windows floating in the air"
    type: "Semi-transparent interface"
    shape: "Wide screen with gentle curves"
    content: "A colorful list is visible, transparently, within the window."
    details: "Since the window (display) is semi-transparent, the character and background behind it are visible through it"

## Background and Environment
environment:
  setting: "Abstract and minimal cyberspace"
  background:
    color: "Black"
    details:
      - "A white starburst (with very thin, sharp spikes) is drawn behind the character, centered on the character."
      - "Small particles of data light and semi-transparent cubes are slowly drifting around her"
    text:
      - "Upper right of the screen: Large vertical text: 'After all, Sticky ToC....' (The text 'Sticky ToC' should be displayed horizontally.)"
      - "Upper left of the screen: Large vertical text: 'Sticky ToC \n solves everything....!!' (The text 'Sticky ToC' should be displayed horizontally.)"

## Art Style and Quality
style:
  art_style: "High-quality anime illustration, smooth line art and vibrant colors"
  lighting: "The character herself and the window (display) she is operating are the main light sources. Soft reflected light from the display hits her face and body. Overall bright and clean impression."
  color_palette: "White base, with pastel pink, emerald green, cyber blue, and cyan as accent colors"
  effects: "Moderate use of glow and bloom effects"
  quality: "Highest quality, masterpiece, ultra-high resolution, detailed"
```

### No. 120: Game Asset - Bioluminescent Archivist Sci-Fi Portrait Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed JSON prompt for generating a hyper-realistic, cinematic sci-fi portrait of a subject (The Protagonist) in a cluttered exo-botany research station, featuring glowing cyan veins (practical effect makeup) and dramatic magenta rim lighting, simulating a Hasselblad camera shot.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "vibe_title_en": "Bioluminescent Archivist",
  "master_prompt": "A hyper-realistic, cinematic close-up of The Protagonist situated in a claustrophobic, cluttered exo-botany research station. The subject looks directly into the lens with a piercing, intense gaze. The skin is textured with hyper-detailed 'practical effect' glowing veins and circuitry patterns that emit a soft cyan luminescence, appearing as applied UV-reactive makeup rather than CGI. Sweat and humidity are visible on the pores. The shoulders are encased in a rough, tactile armor made of slate shards and woven fiber-optic cables. The background is an incredibly busy, dense mess of hanging alien flora, dripping condensation, scattered glass specimen jars, and disorganized research notes, creating a 'lived-in' scientific chaos. Lighting is a dramatic mix of cool cyan ambient bioluminescence and a sharp magenta rim light cutting through the volumetric haze. Shot on a Hasselblad H6D-100c with an 80mm f/1.9 lens to capture the micro-texture of the glowing skin against the cluttered depth.",
  "meta": {
    "intent": "Cinematic Portraiture",
    "priorities": "Photorealism, Texture, Surreal Lighting",
    "device_profile": "Hasselblad H6D-100c"
  },
  "frame": {
    "aspect": "4:5",
    "composition": "Centralized close-up with cluttered depth layering",
    "layout": "Portrait",
    "camera_angle": "Eye-level, slightly angled",
    "tilt_roll_degrees": "0"
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "Female",
    "identity": "The Protagonist",
    "demographics": "Universal/Ambiguous",
    "face": "Intense gaze, hyper-realistic skin texture, wetness from humidity",
    "hair": "Braided or textured, interwoven with thin wires or vines",
    "body": "Shoulders visible, posture tense",
    "expression": "Piercing, mysterious, focused",
    "pose": "Direct engagement with the lens, slight turn of the head"
  },
  "wardrobe_accessories": {
    "garments": [
      {
        "item": "Symbiotic Armor",
        "material": "Slate, Rock, Fiber-optics",
        "color": "Dark Grey with Cyan accents",
        "fit": "Structured, Organic fit"
      }
    ],
    "accessories": [
      {
        "item": "Embedded Circuitry Makeup",
        "color": "{argument name="makeup color" default="Glowing Cyan/Blue"}",
        "material": "UV Reactive Paint/Prosthetic",
        "brand_style": "Sci-Fi Practical Effect"
      }
    ]
  },
  "environment": {
    "setting": "Subterranean Exo-Botany Lab",
    "surfaces": "Glass, wet metal, organic leaves, paper stacks",
    "depth": "Shallow depth of field, cluttered bokeh",
    "atmosphere": "Humid, hazy, dripping wet",
    "lens_interaction": "Slight condensation on lens, blooming highlights"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "key": "Soft Cyan Bioluminescence (from subject/plants)",
    "fill": "Deep Blue ambient",
    "rim": "Sharp Magenta/Pink kicker light",
    "shadows": "Deep, crushed blacks for contrast",
    "color_temperature": "Cool (3200K mixe"
  }
}

## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-nano-banana-pro-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
